  .linkify {
    display: inline;
    padding: 0;

  }
  a:hover, .linkify:hover {
    text-decoration: underline;

  a.button, .button {
    /* Links that look like buttons. */

    align-items: center;

  textarea, select, input {

  }
  /* Note: decoupling heading levels from styles is useful for
  * accessibility because styles will not always line up with semantically

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

Comment 

12



<a class="comment-link" href="?id=1201032#c12">Comment 12<!----></a>



          


        by
        




      

<link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/icon?family=Material+Icons" rel="stylesheet">


      

schedule

<i id="availability-icon" class="material-icons inline-icon ${user.last_visit_timestamp ? '': 'inline-icon-unseen'}" title="undefined" hidden="">schedule</i>


      



pmonette@chromium.org



<a id="user-link" href="/u/888900135" title="pmonette@chromium.org"><!---->pmonette@chromium.org<!----></a>


      



pmonette@chromium.org



<span id="user-text" hidden=""><!---->pmonette@chromium.org<!----></span>


      





<div id="availability-text" class="availability-notice" title="undefined" hidden=""><!----><!----></div>


    



<mr-user-link></mr-user-link>


        on
        




      

Fri, Apr 30, 2021, 2:11 AM EDT


    



<chops-timestamp title="Fri, Apr 30, 2021, 2:11 AM EDT"></chops-timestamp>


        




      


        

<div>
          <a class="comment-link" href="?id=1201032#c12">Comment 12<!----></a>

          
        by
        <mr-user-link></mr-user-link>
        on
        <chops-timestamp title="Fri, Apr 30, 2021, 2:11 AM EDT"></chops-timestamp>
        
      
        </div>


        




      

<div role="heading" class="comment-header" aria-level="2">
        <div>
          <a class="comment-link" href="?id=1201032#c12">Comment 12<!----></a>

          
        by
        <mr-user-link></mr-user-link>
        on
        <chops-timestamp title="Fri, Apr 30, 2021, 2:11 AM EDT"></chops-timestamp>
        
      
        </div>
        
      </div>


    


      


        




        


      


        









It's totally normal that the crash is happening in the browser process, because the issue is with the class used to start the select file dialog process from the browser process. I didn't touch the interface of SelectFileDialog when I made the out-of-process file dialogs change.



<span class="line"><!---->It's totally normal that the crash is happening in the browser process, because the issue is with the class used to start the select file dialog process from the browser process. I didn't touch the interface of SelectFileDialog when I made the out-of-process file dialogs change.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





I am definitely not a security expert so don't take this at face value but I think there's no real exploit here. It is my understanding that the "getDownloadLocationText" javascript function is only exposed to WebUI pages,  and there's no way to have third-party code running in those pages, short of using DevTools, which I don't think we're explicitely guarding agaisnt. 



<span class="line"><!---->I am definitely not a security expert so don't take this at face value but I think there's no real exploit here. It is my understanding that the "getDownloadLocationText" javascript function is only exposed to WebUI pages,  and there's no way to have third-party code running in those pages, short of using DevTools, which I don't think we're explicitely guarding agaisnt. <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





I don't fully understand the downloads page code, so I'm not sure if this is a real bug that can be hit with some sequence of action on the part of the user, but I've taken a look at the SelectFileDialog interface and I think its design is somewhat flawed, making it very easy to misuse it.



<span class="line"><!---->I don't fully understand the downloads page code, so I'm not sure if this is a real bug that can be hit with some sequence of action on the part of the user, but I've taken a look at the SelectFileDialog interface and I think its design is somewhat flawed, making it very easy to misuse it.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This is how it's supposed to be used:



<span class="line"><!---->This is how it's supposed to be used:<!----></span>



<br>





You make your class extend SelectFileDialog::Listener. You call SelectFileDialog::Create() that takes "this" as a parameter which returns a scoped_refptr to a ref-counted SelectFileDialog instance. The object is ref-counted so even if you get rid of the one reference you own, the instance will still exist and complete its work. You are supposed to manually call OnListenerDestroyed() when you are done with the SelectFileDialog instance, presumably because this usually only happens when your class gets destroyed.



<span class="line"><!---->You make your class extend SelectFileDialog::Listener. You call SelectFileDialog::Create() that takes "this" as a parameter which returns a scoped_refptr to a ref-counted SelectFileDialog instance. The object is ref-counted so even if you get rid of the one reference you own, the instance will still exist and complete its work. You are supposed to manually call OnListenerDestroyed() when you are done with the SelectFileDialog instance, presumably because this usually only happens when your class gets destroyed.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This manual step should actually be called everytime you get rid of your reference to the SelectFileDialog, not just when the listener is destroyed. I think this is error-prone and the name of the method is misleading.



<span class="line"><!---->This manual step should actually be called everytime you get rid of your reference to the SelectFileDialog, not just when the listener is destroyed. I think this is error-prone and the name of the method is misleading.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





My opinion is that the solution would be to make SelectFileDialog::Create return a unique_ptr instead of a ref-counted object which, when deleted, would itself tell the ref-counted object that the listener is no longer listening. The implementation could still use a ref-counted object internally. This will require a little bit of refactoring to the SelectFileDialog code and its users.



<span class="line"><!---->My opinion is that the solution would be to make SelectFileDialog::Create return a unique_ptr instead of a ref-counted object which, when deleted, would itself tell the ref-counted object that the listener is no longer listening. The implementation could still use a ref-counted object internally. This will require a little bit of refactoring to the SelectFileDialog code and its users.<!----></span>

That's because the functions are all bounded to a button, which cannot be hit again while the file dialog is open. That's because the SelectFileDialog code ensures that the window is disabled for the duration of the select file operation (at least on Windows, using

One last comment. The proposed patch for the ImportDataHandler is not adequate because it breakes the "Choose File" button after the first click. So if the user clicks on Choose File, cancels the dialog, and then tries again, the button will simply not do anything. This is certainly not the intended behavior.

The extension is only required for the three vulnerabilities "1.DownloadsHandler_uaf_demo", "2.ImportDataHandler_uaf_demo" and "4.NewTabPageHandler_uaf_demo". The remaining "3.SearchTabHelper_uaf_demo" and "5.PolicyUIHandler_uaf_demo" do not require the extension.



<span class="line"><!---->The extension is only required for the three vulnerabilities "1.DownloadsHandler_uaf_demo", "2.ImportDataHandler_uaf_demo" and "4.NewTabPageHandler_uaf_demo". The remaining "3.SearchTabHelper_uaf_demo" and "5.PolicyUIHandler_uaf_demo" do not require the extension.<!----></span>

Hi amyressler@, additional explanations of the new POCs in 



<span class="line"><!---->Hi amyressler@, additional explanations of the new POCs in <!----></span>





Comment 39



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="#c39"><!---->Comment 39<!----></a>





 are below.



<span class="line"><!----> are below.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





In "1.DownloadsHandler_uaf_demo", "2.ImportDataHandler_uaf_demo" and "4.NewTabPageHandler_uaf_demo", the extension api chrome.tabs.move was used to trigger vulnerabilities without dev tools.



<span class="line"><!---->In "1.DownloadsHandler_uaf_demo", "2.ImportDataHandler_uaf_demo" and "4.NewTabPageHandler_uaf_demo", the extension api chrome.tabs.move was used to trigger vulnerabilities without dev tools.<!----></span>



<br>





In 



<span class="line"><!---->In <!----></span>





Comment #13



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="#c13"><!---->Comment #13<!----></a>





, pmonette@ described that the SelectFileDialog code ensures that the window is disabled for the duration of the select file operation. To bypass the disabled window, the tab existing in the disabled window is moved to another window using the "chrome.tabs.move" api so that the select file operation can be performed again.



<span class="line"><!---->, pmonette@ described that the SelectFileDialog code ensures that the window is disabled for the duration of the select file operation. To bypass the disabled window, the tab existing in the disabled window is moved to another window using the "chrome.tabs.move" api so that the select file operation can be performed again.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





In "3.SearchTabHelper_uaf_demo" and "5.PolicyUIHandler_uaf_demo", Chrome's "tab-search" function was used to close the tabs in the disabled window by the select file operation.



<span class="line"><!---->In "3.SearchTabHelper_uaf_demo" and "5.PolicyUIHandler_uaf_demo", Chrome's "tab-search" function was used to close the tabs in the disabled window by the select file operation.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The explanation of root causes for all vulnerabilities is the same as in the original report.



<span class="line"><!---->The explanation of root causes for all vulnerabilities is the same as in the original report.<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->Prevent dangling reference possibility<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





SelectFileDialog::Listener interface receives selected file path



<span class="line"><!---->SelectFileDialog::Listener interface receives selected file path<!----></span>



<br>





as const reference in FileSelected(). Depending on implementation



<span class="line"><!---->as const reference in FileSelected(). Depending on implementation<!----></span>



<br>





of particular SelectFileDialog it may or may not be reference to dialog



<span class="line"><!---->of particular SelectFileDialog it may or may not be reference to dialog<!----></span>



<br>





object field.



<span class="line"><!---->object field.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





DownloadsHandler creates select_folder_dialog_, receives selected file



<span class="line"><!---->DownloadsHandler creates select_folder_dialog_, receives selected file<!----></span>



<br>





path reference and destroys dialog before passing reference further.



<span class="line"><!---->path reference and destroys dialog before passing reference further.<!----></span>



<br>





It might cause dangling ref in case dialog implementation changes and



<span class="line"><!---->It might cause dangling ref in case dialog implementation changes and<!----></span>



<br>





it prevents from using current implementation of FakeSelectFileDialog



<span class="line"><!---->it prevents from using current implementation of FakeSelectFileDialog<!----></span>



<br>





with DownloadsHandler.



<span class="line"><!---->with DownloadsHandler.<!----></span>

 Passing variable by value



<span class="line"><!----> Passing variable by value<!----></span>



<br>





to listeners rather than by reference should eliminate root cause, so



<span class="line"><!---->to listeners rather than by reference should eliminate root cause, so<!----></span>
